Ş. | LinkedIn‘de 3.893 takipçi In every bit of communication. | ETK Kablo, whichs main principle is quality, is founded in 1979 in Istanbul, Türkiye to manufacture telephone cables. ETK Kablo became a global leading manufacturer and exporter of low current and fiber optic cables within years, correctly applied the reshaped needs with its completely computer aided machinery, expert and experienced personnel abiding to the international standards and norms.
	In the year 2001, ETK Kablo built its fiber optic cable manufacturing facility to adjust the changing and evolving technology and now ETK Kablo has one of the highest capacity on fiber optic cables.">

    <section class="core-section-container

<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              ETK Kablo, whichs main principle is quality, is founded in 1979 in Istanbul, Türkiye to manufacture telephone cables. ETK Kablo became a global leading manufacturer and exporter of low current and fiber optic cables within years, correctly applied the reshaped needs with its completely computer aided machinery, expert and experienced personnel abiding to the international standards and norms.
	In the year 2001, ETK Kablo built its fiber optic cable manufacturing facility to adjust the changing and evolving technology and now ETK Kablo has one of the highest capacity on fiber optic cables. In its current fiber optic cable manufacturing facility, it is capable of manufacturing fiber optic cables up to 432 optical fiber cores, various single mode and various multi-mode, mini, microduct, armored, multi armored, non-metallic armored, single loose tubed, multi loose tubed, tight buffered, hybrid, composite, flame retardant, fire resistant, single jacketed, multi jacketed, messenger wired, all-dielectric self-supporting (ADSS), other various types according to the customer specifications.
	ETK Kablo has a global and respectable place, with the principles of correct product, correct time and correct price, just in time delivery, perfectness, minimum waste, strong pre-sales and after-sales activities, continuous improvement, environmentally-conscious, respectful to the employee rights, utmost occupational safety in its presence in more than 120 countries of 5 continents with the principle of quality first on all of its products and services.
          </p>

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌟 Have you ever wondered how a high-quality cable is made? 🌟

At ETK Kablo, every meter of cable tells a story of precision, innovation, and commitment. Here's a glimpse into the journey of a cable, from concept to completion:

1️⃣ Design &amp; R&amp;D: Our team begins by crafting the perfect specifications tailored to meet the unique needs of our clients.

 2️⃣ Manufacturing: Utilizing advanced technology, such as our recently installed <a class="link" href="https://at.linkedin.com/company/rosendahl---cable-&amp;-wire-manufacturing-solutions?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Rosendahl - Cable &amp; Wire Manufacturing Solutions</a> and <a class="link" href="https://fr.linkedin.com/company/setic-pourtier?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SETIC, POURTIER &amp; C2S</a> machines, we ensure every cable is crafted with perfection.

 3️⃣ Quality Control: In our newly renovated fully equipped laboratory, each product undergoes rigorous testing to meet global standards.

 4️⃣ Delivery: From our facilities to over 120 countries worldwide, we ensure timely delivery and exceptional customer support.

This behind-the-scenes process is our way of ensuring that every cable carries the promise of excellence, reliability, and sustainability. 🌍

💬 What part of this process excites you the most? Let us know in the comments!

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">☎️ Before Wi-Fi, before Fiber… we all started here.

From childhood toy phones to today’s global telecom networks, telephone cables have always been the original network heroes.

At ETK Kablo, we continue this legacy by manufacturing telephone cables that ensure:

 ✔️ Reliable voice transmission
 ✔️ Long-lasting performance
 ✔️ Compliance with international standards

Technologies evolve, but trust in the line remains timeless.

We are proud to announce that ETK Kablo has been recognized among Turkey’s Top 500 IT Companies 2024 in the research conducted by <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/bthabergazetesi?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>BThaber Gazetesi</a>.

We sincerely thank our passionate team, trusted partners, and valued customers who made this achievement possible. Together, we will continue to connect the world, one cable at a time. 🌍✨

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚨 Big News at ETK Kablo! 

We’re proud to announce that our data cable portfolio has officially received the B2ca, s1a, d1, a1 certificate – one of the highest European CPR classifications for reaction to fire. 🎉

What does this mean? 

It means safer buildings, trusted performance, and cables that don’t just carry data… they carry confidence.

Certified product families include:

 • Cat 6 F/FTP
 • Cat 6A F/FTP
 • Cat 6 F/UTP
 • Cat 6A F/UTP
 • Cat 6 U/FTP
 • Cat 6A U/FTP
 • Cat 6 U/UTP
 • Cat 6A U/UTP

In short: whether you twist, shield, foil, or pair them – we’ve got them all covered… literally 😉.

This certification is another milestone in ETK Kablo’s mission to deliver safe, high-performance, and globally compliant cables to projects in more than 120 countries. 🌍

Here’s to faster data, safer networks, and maybe one day… fewer acronyms? (But let’s be honest, we kind of love them).

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">💪 Steel Strength, Fiber Speed: ETK Kablo’s Steel Wire Armored Fiber Optic Cables
 
At ETK Kablo, we take pride in delivering fiber optic solutions that combine maximum protection with uncompromised performance.
 
Our Steel Wire Armored (SWA) Fiber Optic Cables are engineered for the most demanding environments, ensuring:

 ✅ Superior mechanical protection against impact and rodent attacks
 ✅ Reliable performance in harsh outdoor conditions
 ✅ High tensile strength for direct burial and industrial applications
 ✅ Wide fiber options (Singlemode G.652D, G.657A1/A2 and Multimode  OM1–OM5)
 ✅ Compliance with international standards for long-term durability
 
With exports to more than 120 countries across 5 continents, ETK Kablo stands as a trusted global manufacturer — proudly representing Türkiye in the world of advanced cabling.

Whether for telecom networks, data centers, or critical infrastructure projects, our armored fiber optic cables provide the resilience and stability your networks demand.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Building More Capacity With Less Cable ⚡

ETK Kablo’s flex-module fiber optic cables pair G.657.A2 bend-insensitive fibers with kink-resistant mini-modules to protect performance in tight pathways.

The result → high fiber density for better duct utilization and lower civil works, plus a lighter, more manageable cable for faster pulls.

Key Advantages:

 ✅ Bend-insensitive performance: stable attenuation in confined routes
 ✅ Kink-resistant modules: helps avoid micro-bends and signal loss
 ✅ High-density architecture: more fibers per duct, smaller outer diameters
 ✅ Easy handling: smaller, lighter, more flexible construction
 ✅ Tool-free access: modules open cleanly for rapid fiber prep

ETK Kablo manufactures to international standards and tailors designs to your project’s route, duct, and CPR requirements. 🌍

👉 Learn more: <a class="link" href="http://www.etkkablo.com?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>www.etkkablo.com</a>
</p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🔥 Myth vs. Fact 🔥

❌ Myth: “All cables stop working during a fire.”

✅ Fact: Fire-resistant cables, like ETK’s FE180 / PH120 designs, are engineered to maintain circuit integrity even under extreme fire conditions. These cables ensure that emergency lighting, alarms, and critical communication systems continue to operate when they are needed most.

While standard cables can fail within minutes of exposure to flames, fire-resistant cables are tested to withstand fire for up to 180 minutes—providing life-saving reliability in hospitals, airports, tunnels, and high-rise buildings. 

At ETK Kablo, we don’t just design cables to connect the world—we design them to protect it. 🌍

👉 For more information: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/drDpjiRu?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/drDpjiRu</a></p>
